# ListObjectVersions — результаты тестов

**Дата:** 2026-03-23 15:02:48
**Region:** `us-east-1`
**Bucket:** `test-dagm-bucket-listversioning`

---

## 2. Невалидный max-keys

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **400** |
| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |
| Error Message | **Provided max-keys not an integer or within integer range** |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&max-keys=abc`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<Error>
  <Code>InvalidArgument</Code>
  <Message>Provided max-keys not an integer or within integer range</Message>
  <ArgumentName>max-keys</ArgumentName>
  <ArgumentValue>abc</ArgumentValue>
  <RequestId>3ZV49MBJ220J81MY</RequestId>
  <HostId>CGD1OQA66zTbBYieIe8CyBifPxVkheHo0NWAiAZOA11F31fI/Z1WC4qbBXw2cX40HlZjapEbzq5kKKqVOi3Y3mWZDdaO0bvT</HostId>
</Error>
```

## 4. Невалидный encoding-type

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **400** |
| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |
| Error Message | **Invalid Encoding Method specified in Request** |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&encoding-type=invalid-encoding`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<Error>
  <Code>InvalidArgument</Code>
  <Message>Invalid Encoding Method specified in Request</Message>
  <ArgumentName>encoding-type</ArgumentName>
  <ArgumentValue>invalid-encoding</ArgumentValue>
  <RequestId>AVJD76V3T20VDHW5</RequestId>
  <HostId>D2kJqF2gSYc0qWwi5mqVKWUV6NyzKPnUELIF2uCgyVScQRujcb7kO144aTSLgc2xCT1fBZhcfYs=</HostId>
</Error>
```

## 6. version-id-marker без key-marker

|---|---|

| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |

```xml
</Error>
```

## 12. Пагинация key-marker без version-id-marker

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **200** |
| MaxKeys | 1 |
| IsTruncated | true |
| NextKeyMarker | `b` |
| Versions | 1 |
| DeleteMarkers | 0 |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&key-marker=ab&max-keys=1`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<ListVersionsResult xmlns="http://s3.amazonaws.com/doc/2006-03-01/">
  <Name>test-dagm-bucket-listversioning</Name>
  <Prefix/>
  <KeyMarker>ab</KeyMarker>
  <VersionIdMarker/>
  <NextKeyMarker>b</NextKeyMarker>
  <NextVersionIdMarker>l_frwiZPBYGjp6saPiVPEwc4F3YzspXF</NextVersionIdMarker>
  <MaxKeys>1</MaxKeys>
  <IsTruncated>true</IsTruncated>
  <Version>
    <Key>b</Key>
    <VersionId>l_frwiZPBYGjp6saPiVPEwc4F3YzspXF</VersionId>
    <IsLatest>true</IsLatest>
    <LastModified>2026-03-23T13:01:38.000Z</LastModified>
    <ETag>"e307ad3ba6afd0088dbc8afcfeb56209"</ETag>
    <ChecksumAlgorithm>CRC32</ChecksumAlgorithm>
    <ChecksumType>FULL_OBJECT</ChecksumType>
    <Size>16</Size>
    <Owner>
      <ID>10adec58aa82e4276fcd6bffd437ba0e42ae890098cf4bba7aa0aa8215241bfd</ID>
    </Owner>
    <StorageClass>STANDARD</StorageClass>
  </Version>
</ListVersionsResult>
```

## 13. Пагинация key-marker + version-id-marker=null

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **200** |
| MaxKeys | 1 |
| IsTruncated | true |
| NextKeyMarker | `a/` |
| Versions | 1 |
| DeleteMarkers | 0 |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&key-marker=a&version-id-marker=null&max-keys=1`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<ListVersionsResult xmlns="http://s3.amazonaws.com/doc/2006-03-01/">
  <Name>test-dagm-bucket-listversioning</Name>
  <Prefix/>
  <KeyMarker>a</KeyMarker>
  <VersionIdMarker>null</VersionIdMarker>
  <NextKeyMarker>a/</NextKeyMarker>
  <NextVersionIdMarker>TnIFQsALePIyQXJeK_n4_wgtAqVV9q_k</NextVersionIdMarker>
  <MaxKeys>1</MaxKeys>
  <IsTruncated>true</IsTruncated>
  <Version>
    <Key>a/</Key>
    <VersionId>TnIFQsALePIyQXJeK_n4_wgtAqVV9q_k</VersionId>
    <IsLatest>true</IsLatest>
    <LastModified>2026-03-23T13:01:37.000Z</LastModified>
    <ETag>"d012122e169f75f9430d6907ab4c65be"</ETag>
    <ChecksumAlgorithm>CRC32</ChecksumAlgorithm>
    <ChecksumType>FULL_OBJECT</ChecksumType>
    <Size>17</Size>
    <Owner>
      <ID>10adec58aa82e4276fcd6bffd437ba0e42ae890098cf4bba7aa0aa8215241bfd</ID>
    </Owner>
    <StorageClass>STANDARD</StorageClass>
  </Version>
</ListVersionsResult>
```

## P1. Порядок: max-keys=abc + key=k,vid=""

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **400** |
| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |
| Error Message | **Provided max-keys not an integer or within integer range** |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&max-keys=abc&key-marker=k&version-id-marker=`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<Error>
  <Code>InvalidArgument</Code>
  <Message>Provided max-keys not an integer or within integer range</Message>
  <ArgumentName>max-keys</ArgumentName>
  <ArgumentValue>abc</ArgumentValue>
  <RequestId>D4EMB00KNVHXS098</RequestId>
  <HostId>t+T2KD91N47AGlaeYNRDITObyEdkMdZLAnLuG3P8AI9Z5hA8p4IhD77LZ9yUPrp+b2hqIkrkLYk=</HostId>
</Error>
```

---

## P2. Порядок: key=k,vid="" + encoding=invalid

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **400** |
| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |
| Error Message | **A version-id marker cannot be empty.** |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&key-marker=k&version-id-marker=&encoding-type=invalid`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<Error>
  <Code>InvalidArgument</Code>
  <Message>A version-id marker cannot be empty.</Message>
  <ArgumentName>version-id-marker</ArgumentName>
  <ArgumentValue/>
  <RequestId>SYK777H9H7Q5CX08</RequestId>
  <HostId>NfaMnNDdxXZpMyMFcj9zFyRxR+4PZwGF9Q/gYd1oIncd39Ag1I+0SxnqOSUJIpW1EruJqFb0hklnVVIptH3UDhf5dkPcaPJa</HostId>
</Error>
```

---

## P3. Порядок: vid="" без key

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **400** |
| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |
| Error Message | **A version-id marker cannot be specified without a key marker.** |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&version-id-marker=`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<Error>
  <Code>InvalidArgument</Code>
  <Message>A version-id marker cannot be specified without a key marker.</Message>
  <ArgumentName>version-id-marker</ArgumentName>
  <ArgumentValue/>
  <RequestId>WFZSVEV2J4S5H6TP</RequestId>
  <HostId>G3oEMJ6nOux/9Dy3YrT2Sj7UoAXsbyYU5SwAdtF7bdN4IVVhScpNDQVvzeYTze5j+XqdEELJtUyxYnu/gK2jhg==</HostId>
</Error>
```

---

## P4. Порядок: vid=bad + encoding=invalid без key

| | Тест |
|---|---|
| Status | **400** |
| Error Code | **InvalidArgument** |
| Error Message | **A version-id marker cannot be specified without a key marker.** |

**Запрос:** `GET /{bucket}?versions&version-id-marker=bad-vid&encoding-type=invalid`

**Ответ:**

```xml
<Error>
  <Code>InvalidArgument</Code>
  <Message>A version-id marker cannot be specified without a key marker.</Message>
  <ArgumentName>version-id-marker</ArgumentName>
  <ArgumentValue>bad-vid</ArgumentValue>
  <RequestId>AV6M1HNCQ0DTPP3E</RequestId>
  <HostId>vfHdnmlU27ueFEqvd/6gzKYO4jBTGLRx8EQ98BxrXOoqVGKVmmRm0NcBHxHtFN5MKYfwj410rHI=</HostId>
</Error>
```

## P6. Порядок: max-keys=abc + vid=bad без key

```xml
</Error>
```
